You wait for a while.....and a couple of minutes of time go by without you doing anything.

> follow other mercenaries
You follow the other two mercenaries, who go into the High Castle. They don't go very far before they take up position outside a doorway. You hide behind a convenient pillar from where you can plan your next move.

Behind Pillar
You are hiding behind a pillar in a vaulted corridor in the High Castle. At the North end of the corridor, about seven metres away, there is a carved archway framing an arched double door. The corridor also leads South to the courtyard outside.  Standing guard in front of the arched door to the north are two mercenaries.

> throw dagger at tall mercenary
You step from behind the pillar and throw your dagger at the tall mercenary. It gets him right in the throat and his eyes go wide with shock. He drops his lochaber axe, which falls to the ground with a long clang, and he reaches up and pulls the dagger out of his throat.

This, however, only makes the wound worse and great gouts of blood spurt from the severed artery. The dagger falls from lifeless fingers and his body falls to the ground with a heavy thud. It twitches a couple of times and then there is silence.

The short mercenary is momentarily stunned by his comrades' death but then he sees you standing by the pillar and he yells in rage. Drawing his rapier, he runs towards you, shouting curses in his own language. You cannot understand him but you assume they are not complimentary.

You engage his rapier with your longsword and battle commences! He is a very good swordsman but you are his match and the longer reach of your sword begins to tell as you inflict minor wounds on his body.

He eventually starts to tire and you end the fight by parrying a thrust from his rapier and thrusting with your sword to take him in the chest. His eyes go wide with shock and he slides backwards off your blade to lie dead on the ground!

By Pointed Archway
You are standing in front of a pointed archway in which there are double doors. You can go South along the corridor to the pillar where you were hiding, or East through the doors.  Lying sprawled on the floor here are the bodies of the two mercenaries who were guarding the doors.  Also here is a dagger, a rapier and a lochaber axe.

> open doors
You open the arched doors.

> drop all
Ok, you put down the large shield, the lantern, the square of calfskin, the long sword and the small, clay pot.

> get shield
Ok, you pick up the large shield.

> e
You move east.

West End of Church
You're at the West End of St.Mary's Church, in the nave. The vaulted ceiling is intricately carved and painted with biblical scenes, and the walls are festooned with the battle flags of the various "houses" of the Teutonic Order. On either side of the aisle are rows of pews and the walls are hung with tapestries. The sanctuary is East, the corridor West through the double doors underneath the pointed archway.

You hear a voice from from the other end of the church and look in that direction to see that there is someone sitting in the Bishop's throne - it is the sorcerer-prince himself, Wladyslaw.

He utters a curse in a language you do not know then leaps up from the chair and stands there with a furious look on his face. You realise with surprise that Wladyslaw is only a small man - you expected someone about three metres tall and covered in hair. He wears a long black cloak and his long hair falls either side of his scarred face in tight curls.

"How the hell did you get past my guards!?" he shouts in a heavily-accented voice. "I trust they have paid with their lives for their incompetence? I suppose you think that you are going to finish me off just as easily?

He draws himself up to his full height then, muttering the words of an incantation, launches a spell at you which hurtles towards you in a shower of incandescent sparks!

You instinctively raise your shield to protect yourself and it deflects the spell away.

The sorcerer then launches a series of increasingly powerful disabling spells at you that threaten to knock the shield from your arm. You suddenly realise that the bolts of arcane energy are bouncing off the mirror you fixed to the front of your shield!

You hold your shield in front of you with both hands and advance towards the sorcerer, whose mouth gapes open and his eyes go wide with surprise.

"See how you deal with this, then," he snarls and he mutters the incantation for the most powerful death spell he knows. Flinging his arms at you he casts the spell, which roars through the air towards you.

You are only a couple of metres from him as the spell hits your shield. It hits the mirror square-on and rebounds off the mirror in a shower of deep red sparks. You hear a scream of "NO....!" which is cut off abruptly as the spell hits Wladyslaw straight in the face, killing him instantly.

He collapses to the floor of the church and you lower your shield to gaze upon his body. As you watch with horror, his skin starts to wrinkle and his body shrinks in upon itself as the spell which prolonged his life fades away. The skin eventually sloughs away from the sorcerer's bones, which themselves then start to crumble away. Soon, all that is left of Wladyslaw is his cloak and a pile of dust.

The Crossing
You are in the Crossing of the church where, on the left side, steps lead Up to the pulpit, while opposite that is the Bishop's throne where Wladyslaw was sitting. The trancepts are to the North and South and the Nave is West.  Also here is the sorcerer's cloak and a pile of dust.

> find bell tower entrance
You look around the church and try to find the entrance to the bell tower. Eventually you notice the edge of a door peeping out from behind the side of one of the tapestries hanging on the north wall.

West End of Church
You're at the West End of St.Mary's Church, in the nave. The vaulted ceiling is intricately carved and painted with biblical scenes, and the walls are festooned with the battle flags of the various "houses" of the Teutonic Order. On either side of the aisle are rows of pews and the walls are hung with tapestries. The sanctuary is East, the corridor West through the double doors underneath the pointed archway and there is a door leading North behind one of the tapestries.

> open bell tower door
You open the Bell Tower door.

> run up stairs
You go to run through the door when you are startled by a shout from behind you.

"Oii! Get away from that door!"

You look around to see the one remaining mercenary standing in the doorway at the west end of the church! He starts to run towards you, his longsword at the ready. You run through the doorway and up the stairs to the belfry as fast as your legs will carry you, the mercenary in hot pursuit.

The Ringing Room
You are in the bell ringing room, where the bell ropes hang down through two square holes in the wooden ceiling. The only exit is a door that leads Down the spiral stairway outside.  The boards of the floor are bare of any covering and the only comfort is the old chair that stands in one corner.

You can hear the mercenary running up the stairs - he will be here in seconds!

> wedge door with chair
You slam the door shut and, grabbing the chair, you wedge the back of it under the handle and the legs against the edge of one of the floorboards - it should hold the door shut but not for very long!

The Ringing Room

The mercenary is outside trying to break down the door!
